# 36 - Half A Month Has Passed Since Then

Half a month had already passed since the dramatic return from the Marra Dungeon. We safely returned to the slum and immediately headed to the Guild to report everything. Alex’s group’s survival, the discovery of the deep layer of the Marra Dungeon, the monsters that appeared there, and the magic civilization mechanisms that could be called Marra’s legacy—each of these was big news.

Himmler winced as he listened to the report, despite his excitement.

The look on his face showed that he was troubled because he couldn’t read what decision the higher-ups would make after hearing this report. Well, his troubles were none of my business.

Marī and I were handed a considerable reward as an interim payment for the complete achievement of the quest. Himmler’s statement was that since the Silver Rank Party had returned, they would likely receive a suitable reward from the nobility later on.

Several things became clear during this half-month regarding the events that occurred in the Dungeon.

One was the reason Marī was able to escape before us.

After being moved to the Inner Dungeon by the teleporter, she immediately began exploring the Dungeon on her own. Her magical approach, which was skilled in mana detection, seemed to have paid off; the truth was that she quickly found a teleporter that returned to the original location and was able to get back to the Base.

However, there was no sign of my return at the Base outside the Dungeon.

Sensing that I had gone into the depths of the Dungeon by using the teleporter—she apparently didn’t know how I activated the device—to follow Marī, she decided to wait for me at the Base for only one week, the limit of their food and water.

And when she noticed the loud noise and vibration caused by the activation of the device, she cautiously peered outside, only to run right into us as we were escaping the Dungeon.

The second was about the nobleman’s son.

This was casually revealed by the person himself at a post town we stopped at on the way home. The person was, as expected, Alex. I think being of noble blood is quite a secret, and I don’t think he should have nonchalantly revealed it in the communal bath, even if we had the place reserved.

Well, in any case, Alex was the nobleman’s son in question.

He didn’t seem to have reached a conclusion within himself yet about whether he would continue as an adventurer or retire.

By the way, he explained the reason for confiding in me:

“I dragged you into my personal affairs, after all. It wouldn’t be fair to keep secrets from a comrade, would it?”

“That’s an incomprehensible logic.”

“Heh heh, is that so? I feel like I could tell you anything now—Zarumen. How about it? Are you interested in my secret?”

“No, I’m not. Ask Clair or someone else to listen to that.”

“…Tch, you’re an uncooperative fellow…”

He said that, but Alex was wearing an openhearted smile. I somehow felt like the distance between him and me had shortened compared to the old days, and I… w-well, it’s not like I was happy about getting along with another guy or anything!? This was why I couldn’t stand genuinely handsome guys!

Marī said that the old me was quite “something,” but if you asked me, Alex was the one who was “something.” He had a sweet face, graceful manners, high skill, and a free-spirited personality—he’s specced like a biological weapon with full gigolo elements, yet I’ve never heard a single rumor of him having a steady relationship. Basically, all the stories were about which woman was infatuated with him, and not a single piece of decisive information about him dating someone has come out.

My suspicion that he might prefer men over women only deepened.

The third was about Cindy’s bruises.

The Curse she received apparently wasn’t the kind that would immediately endanger her life.

Marī asserted this, which Clair couldn’t determine. However, no one among us doubted her. There probably aren’t many people who have researched Curses more than she has.

The problem was that the bruises would remain as an after-effect of the Curse.

We were told that a Curse was the malignant resentment of the dead envying the living, which ate away at the body and soul—which sounded horrifying—but Marī said that Cindy’s bruises were a result of damage she received from touching a cursed object that still remained in her body. Apparently, if the purification at the church and the wound healing proceed smoothly, the bruises would eventually fade from sight.

Cindy looked happy when she heard that.

Even though she’s a little shrimp, she’s still very much a woman. Of course, she’d be concerned.

“Zaryū, were you thinking something rude just now?”

“I-Wasn’t-Thinking-Anything.”

“Then, think of Cindy’s sexy body and get excited.”

“Hahaha, that’s absolutely not going to happen.”

“Annoying.”

I was lightly blown away ten meters by Cindy’s angry dropkick.

The Slums didn’t have anything as fancy as a clock tower.

A large, magnificent clock tower reportedly soared in the center of the city, on the other side of that tall wall.

Only the chimes that marked the time were leaping over the cliff-like wall and leaking all the way to the Slums.

The sound of the bell bestowed its grace equally upon the rich and the poor.

# 42 - The Libra Marquis

“My name is Zarumen.”

# 43 - The Fair Harp Tavern

After finishing the meeting with Marquis Iskandar of Libra, I went with Alex to a familiar eating house.

This was the place where we often held celebration parties when Alex’s party and I were together after completing a quest. This time, since we had all safely returned to town, Cindy and Clair suggested we have a party like old times, with me included.

The Fair Harp Tavern, as its name suggested, had a large harp enthroned in the center of the dining area.

This neighborhood, which could be called the Old Slums, had good public safety, so the clientele was also calm, and merchants from other countries also used the place. It seemed the proprietress had been a harp player in her youth, and initially, she had built up the restaurant by selling performances. Thanks to her efforts, it was still a well-known establishment favored by traveling bards.

Bards with confidence in their skills would visit the tavern and perform their poems.

Customers would savor delicious food, using the performance as a side dish.

In this world, where entertainment was scarce, a restaurant that offered a show was quite a status symbol.

Rumors even whispered that eccentric nobles from the city would secretly frequent the place.

“What is it?”

The stern-faced Libra Marquis and the slender Alex didn’t look much alike. I could see the family connection in his sharp eyebrows and eyes, but he might take after his mother more.

“Is that woman so important?”

The monstrous, grotesque creatures, solidified malice itself.

“…What is it?”

The calamity that destroyed the flourishing Marra overnight. It was said that the Marra Dungeon was where the people of Marra fled on the day of the disaster. And it was there that we encountered that horrifying-looking, curse-wielding monster.

Simple-minded me couldn’t help but imagine a dangerous connection there.

I couldn’t believe that the curse plaguing Marī and the curse that injured Cindy were entirely unrelated.

The shadow of a curse clinging to the ruined city of Marra.

We would discover whether a demon or a snake awaited us by exploring the innermost parts of the Marra Dungeon.

The rational part of me criticized my present self, saying I sounded like a rookie Adventurer with a hero complex.

I had seen the demise of many people who overconfidentially reached out for more than they could handle and self-destructed, but I couldn’t tell if the path I was on now was the same as theirs.

I thought I would never have it again.

“Zaryū!” Cindy called out.

“Senior!” Clair called.

“Zarumen!” Marī called.

“Zaryū!” Alex called.

In a chorus. The four people, who had been arguing, suddenly synchronized.

“What is it?”

“Welcome back,” Cindy said.

“Welcome back,” Clair echoed.

“You took too long to come back,” Alex stated.

“We were waiting,” Marī finished.

Mugs in hand were offered to me, who stood there flinching.

I hid my embarrassment by clinking my own mug against theirs, which awaited it in the center of the table.

“I’m home.”

Afterward, the drinking party, with our shared memories from when I was around and the party’s adventures after I left as the side dish, continued until sunset.

“Ehehe~. Senpai~! Let’s drink more!”

Clair, her face bright red, hugged my arm in a cheerful mood.

Her head swayed unsteadily, and her steps were uncertain. She looked like she wouldn’t be able to walk straight unless she clung to my arm. She was perfectly drunk. I knew she wasn’t very good with alcohol, but it was the first time I had seen her this intoxicated.

Even in my past life, where public order was good, leaving a drunken woman alone was dangerous.

In this world, that went without saying. Even if she’s a Silver Rank Adventurer whose physical strength was recognized by the Guild, there were countless ways to harm her.

Looking at the bustling entertainment district, I almost forgot, but this town was ultimately just a part of the Slums. It wouldn’t be strange to hear a scream if you stepped into one of the alleys. The Slums were expanding every year. The more people increased, the worse the public order became.

“I’ll take Clair back to the orphanage.”

My companions immediately nodded at my suggestion.

The gaze of trust they sent my way was both ticklish and comforting.

“Leave Marī and Cindy to me.”

I returned a nod to Alex’s powerful words.

He was the most capable person in this town. There could be no more reliable offer than this.

“Senpai~! Hurry, hurry~!”

“W-Whoa, I got it, just don’t pull!”

I just managed to keep from stumbling as she pulled my arm with more strength than I expected. Even a sister with an adorable appearance, completely unrelated to violence, secretly holds a level nearly twice mine. In a simple test of strength, I was at a disadvantage.

I somehow corrected my posture and walked beside her, who was in a good mood.

She was even humming, “fun fun~,” so she seemed quite delighted.

“Runruru~♪ Ah, look at that stall! They have delicious-looking yakitori! I want to buy some as a souvenir for everyone waiting at the orphanage! That’s okay, right, Senpai!”

“Yes, yes—Uncle, pack up twenty servings of yakitori for me.”

“Aye!”

The friendly smiling Uncle at the stall skillfully wrapped the freshly grilled skewers in large, lotus-like leaves. He tied it with a hemp cord for the finishing touch, creating a simple take-out souvenir from the stall.

“Here, don’t drop it.”

“Ehehe, yes~!”

Clair accepted it happily, wearing an innocent smile.

Where did her usual calm demeanor go? Fortunately, this was the entertainment district in the early evening. There’s no boor who would criticize her, having been led astray by the merriment of the alcohol. If anything, I, whose steps were sure despite leaving a bar, was the strange one for an Adventurer who just returned from a life-or-death quest.

“…Hey, Senpai…”

“What is it?”

A cold night wind blew through.

My left arm, which was touching her, felt unusually hot.

I leaned my ear closer to her voice, which was so tiny it seemed about to vanish into the surrounding din.

“Could I become a prostitute?”

I was speechless at the unexpected question.

Clair becoming a prostitute—the meaning of those words wouldn’t coalesce in my mind.

“If I become a prostitute, can I earn a lot of money?”

“…Is this about managing the orphanage?”

Her hand, which gripped my arm tightly, was faintly trembling.

“It’s not a job where you can earn a lot of money.”

“Why—”

“That alley over there. That shadow moving behind the wooden crate is a streetwalker.”

A shadow wriggling in a dark alley that seemed to melt into the darkness. It was a common spot for a streetwalker’s work at this hour. It was hard to notice amidst the bustle of the main street, but it was a sight commonly seen in alleys here and there.

“The amount changes a bit depending on what you sell, but even so, I don’t think gathering the earnings for one whole night would be enough to buy what you’re holding right now.”

“…Is it that little…”

Clair muttered weakly, dropping her gaze to the souvenirs she was holding.

If you had confidence in your looks, you could take clients to a love hotel.

Of course, there’s also the option of joining a brothel. In terms of earning money you could freely use, taking clients individually brings in more money than joining a brothel. One reason was that a brothel took a large cut, resulting in low profit, but another was simply that joining a brothel meant selling yourself. While you might become a high-class prostitute with money to use freely if you rise up in the brothel, you’d generally be treated as the brothel’s property, so you wouldn’t have any money you could use freely.

“—Besides, taking clients individually carries a huge risk. Financial trouble is a given, you might be subjected to violence and have to suffer in silence, and—in the worst case, the trouble you get into could be life-threatening.”

“…”

“Being an Adventurer is also a dangerous, life-risking job, but if you’re like Clair, a Silver Rank who can use healing magic, I think you’ll get a more stable income by continuing to work as an Adventurer than by becoming a prostitute.”

I tried to say that in a deliberately bright tone, but her face remained dark.

Perhaps, she might have been feigning drunkenness so she could be alone with me to discuss this. The strength with which she was gripping my arm also conveyed how distressed she was. I felt like she might head down a bad path if this continued.

“—That’s right, the next quest looks like it’ll bring in a good amount of money! I’ll give Clair my share of the advance payment for the reward. That way, the orphanage’s finances should be easier for a while, right?”

“Eh?! That’s… but, I can’t accept that… If you did that, I wouldn’t be able to face you, Senpai…”

The look on her face, which suddenly lifted, contained a desperate plea.

She immediately denied the offer, but her true heart was seeking salvation.

“Don’t worry about me. We’ll successfully complete the quest, get a big chunk of the reward… and then you can pay back the loan from the deferred payment. We’re companions, so that’s fine, right?”

It might be inappropriate, but I was a little happy. That Clair had relied on me. With my current Level Up-ed self, I also have the optimistic future projection that I’ll be able to earn a lump sum income as an Adventurer from now on.

“…I’m sorry, Senpai… Thank you… sniff…”

“Hey, hey, don’t cry here!”

Clair clung to my arm, tears streaming down her face.

For a while, until she stopped crying, I would be stared at with indifferent eyes by the passersby.

## The Otherworld Conquest Method of a Reincarnated Porter - Chapter 136 - **Fierce Battle**

Chirp, chirp, chirp.

Since I won’t be able to see Lunamilia for a while, I take the liberty to cum in her mouth once and in her anus twice early in the morning. I was a little too rough, so Lunamilia probably won’t be able to get up for a while. I eat breakfast and, in order to complete the goods transportation request, get ready to head to the territory capital of Breicork.

「Oi, hey, you bastard.」

「Huh? Ah, so it’s you, Gyouza. Do you have a business with me?」

According to what I heard from Ottilie, it seems that Gyouza will also be taking part in this goods transportation request. His storage capacity is 16 barrels, which is quite a lot. Gyouza said he was Cotton Clouds’ exclusive porter, but it seems that’s just a self-proclaimed thing. Cotton Clouds simply hired him in the royal capital for this request.

「It’s not Gyouza, but Gyoza, you bastard! Don’t get cocky just because you can ride a horse.」

I’ve never really bragged about being able to ride a horse, though. Gyouza might have a complex about being the only one who can’t ride a horse. Well, if you’re not of noble birth, you probably won’t have a chance to ride a horse, after all. As fellow porters, I guess I don’t mind teaching him. When we get to the back of the building, Gyouza starts rambling on with veins popping out on his shaved head. He looks like he’s about to use Tri-beam or something.

Crap, I’ve gone and done it now. Gyouza plops down while vomiting and passes out. This is bad, it should be time to gather already. What should I do? 「「「…..」」」

I was wondering what to do if someone were to retort, 「Why did you leave someone else’s party member behind?」, but it seems like no one is concerned about Gyouza. Sylphia raises her hand vigorously and offers to join us as an escort. Why is she being so assertive? This girl, surely she’s not interested in me for real, right? This town is a boring one, so maybe she wants to go shopping in the territory’s capital.

We finish the preparations and set off. The plan is to cross the mountain before the day is over and go to the village where we stayed before. The road connecting the territory capital of Breicork and the border town of Cresar is well sprinkled with holy water, so it seems that you hardly encounter any monsters there. The journey goes smoothly, and when we are about to rest our horses at a base where you can stay the night near the mountaintop, we sense the presence of a large number of people. We keep our distance and watch the situation for a while. It seems that beastfolks are hanging out in the building. I wonder if they’re a bandit band. For better or worse, there should be a caretaker here, so I wonder what has become of them.

One of the beastfolks who have been keeping watch over the surrounding area confirms our presence and hurriedly runs into the building. The boss, or someone of that status, must be in there, and he’s gone to report to him. After a while, a beastfolk with the aura of a powerhouse shows up. It’s a huge, bear-shaped beastfolk, even bigger than the wolfkin from the other day. I don’t mind killing you after torturing and getting the information out of you, but I’d like to save myself the trouble, so if you could just spit it out quickly, that would be a huge help.」

The bearkin man threatens us with a low voice as he glares at us with his glowering big eyes, reminiscent of a yakuza boss. He is unleashing intimidation skill on us. Not good, this guy is very strong.

Everyone gets off their horses and gets ready for battle. The beastfolks standing next to the bearkin man also exude the aura of fairly strong people. A catkin woman wearing gauntlets, a slender foxkin man with sharp eyes, and a dogkin man with two swords hanging from his shoulders. There are about twenty other beastfolks, but the aura around these four is on clearly a different level.

I don’t think Ottilie will lose, but I see no composure in her expression. It seems that she telling us not to lay our hands on him is because she’s worried about us. The beastfolks begin to surround us, and the four strong-looking beastfolks come forward. It seems that the beastfolks around us don’t intend to lay their hands on us. The pairing is decided naturally. The bearkin man and Ottilie, the foxkin man and Sylphia, and then the two adventurers and the dogkin man and catkin women. Laura and Nakulus serve as my guards.

Nakulus, it’s not good to discriminate against beastfolks, you know? Nakulus seems to be superior in terms of provocation skill. Even so, Nakulus has just changed jobs to magic pugilist, so his level shouldn’t be that high yet. That catkin woman seems pretty strong, so I wonder if he’ll be okay.

The dogkin man is yawning, and seems to have plenty of room to spare. Damn it, somehow, I have a bad feeling about this.

It seems that Ottilie has the edge in speed, and even though the bearkin man has only suffered scratches, he is bleeding. After that, an exchange of blows unfolds for a while, but neither of them manages to land a clean hit. However, from the looks of it, I get the feeling that the catkin woman is stronger than Nakulus. Will he be okay?

That foxkin man must have swordsmanship skill of fairly high proficiency level, as he is fighting on equal terms with Sylphia. They are both fighting while probing each other, so it’s hard to tell who is stronger.

「Kuh.」

However, Ottilie, who is channeling magical energy into her sword, should be consuming a lot of magical energy, too. Cotton Clouds is a gold-ranked adventurer party, so she probably has some potions, but the same could be said for her opponent.

Boutos, Age 43, Level 60

Job: Beast Warrior

「Hehehe, farewell, porter.」

Boutos glances at me for a second, then jumps off the mountainside while holding Laura. I hurriedly run to where they’ve fallen and look down, to see that they’re both rolling on the ground as they fall. This slope and the mountainside stretching all the way down. Even if you use body enhancement, you’d be bruised all over your body, so I doubt you’d get out of it scot-free. Boutos, on the verge of death, desperately clings to Laura with the resolve to throw away his own life. Given things, neither of them will be able to properly break the fall, and if they’re hit in the wrong place, the worst could happen. Even if they do survive the fall, it’d be impossible for them to make it back up here in this snow.

Behind me, the battle to the death between Cotton Clouds and the beastfolk bandit band is still unfolding, so I can’t expect any help. Snow is piling up, so I hope it’ll provide a certain degree of cushioning. I wonder if Laura has any potions. In this cold, she’ll probably lose her strength quickly. There’s no time to hesitate. I guess I have no choice but to go. Taking off all my equipment and putting it in my storage to make myself lighter, I head down the slope of the mountainside.

## 137 -  **Conclusion**

The snow started to fall harder, making visibility worse and beginning to pile up. The battlefield was becoming unfavorable for those who fought while making use of their feet. The temperature was falling well below freezing, draining the stamina of those who fought there, but, in the height of a battle to the death, the warriors were moving about furiously and no one paid it any mind.

Nakulus and the male adventurer, who were dealing with the twenty beastfolks, wanted to quickly rout them and go to Ottilie and Sylphia’s aid, but the beastfolks turned out to be way more skilled than they expected, and they were having a hard time.

「Haa, haa, fuhahaha, so strong. I haven’t had a fight this enjoyable since my fight against the Beast King’s brats.」

The bearkin man was breathing heavily and bleeding all over his body, but they were all just scratches. The reason he talked in the middle of the fight was not to buy time, but simply because he was interested in Ottilie, his worthy opponent.

「Phew, the Beast King’s children, is it? If memory serves right, they’re of the lionkin tribe, right? So you must’ve fought them before they grew up and got strong.」

Every time he talked to her, Ottilie also stopped fighting and responded to it. It was not that she was interested in this beastfolk or that she was trying to recover her stamina. It was to set up her magic.

I take it easy on him, but he can’t react at all and ends up getting blown away with a dull thud. A number of teeth also seem to have fallen off. No, this is self-defense, alright? I’m a porter, a non-combatant job, and I’m barehanded, while he’s a knight and he drew his sword. For better or worse, Lunamilia is of noble birth, after all.

「Ugh, gaba, gah…」

「Are you okay, Othniel?」

The young knights around him are looking after the knight called Othniel, who is bleeding from his mouth and writhing in agony. To my surprise, they seem to be giving him a mid-grade red potion. Are they for real? For them to use a potion that costs nearly one large gold coin to buy after only getting punched once. Just how rich are these guys? Even though he’s a knight, is he unable to use healing magic?

「Y, you vashard, how dare you…」

Othniel’s jaw wound has healed completely, but he’s lost a few teeth, so it seems like he’s unable to speak properly. You need a high-grade potion to heal missing body parts, so his teeth haven’t been restored.

Othniel and the others all draw their swords and keep me in check. For ten knights to draw their swords and confront a single porter, don’t they find it embarrassing? Maybe they think I’m a pugilist.

Normally, if I were to take on this many people, I’d lure them into the forest and aim to crush them one by one, but I can’t imagine myself losing at all. After all, even though these guys are ten in number, they don’t even surround me, and are just pointing their swords at me in the same place. Rather than them not intending to fight seriously, I think it’s more of them not knowing how to fight. The only person I need to be wary of, the elderly knight, sighs and looks on from the sidelines with a look of resignation. Now then, what should I do? As they are knights from another country, it’s difficult to deal with them. Even for them, it should be a bad idea to cause bloodshed in another country, but these guys are like shitty young masters who were raised in a pampered manner, and grew into adults as they were. I don’t think we can expect them to think deeply before they act.

「For you to point your swords at God… at Sei-sama, unforgivable. You deserve to die ten thousand deaths.」

Geh, Lunamilia behind me starts to circulate her magical energy. This is bad, sacred magic should be less effective against humans, but the current Lunamilia is capable of using superhuman-class magic. I have to settle this peacefully somehow.

「Hey, you guys, put away your swords. We’ll listen to what you have to say, so…」

「Hmph, looks like you’re getting cold feet. But it’s too late now. You will have to pay for baring your teeth toward us, the knight order of the Holy Kingdom. We’ll send you to the other side, along with that fake saint.」

Damn it, do I have no choice but to do it? Let’s knock them out one by one with my boxing skill. I want to stop Lunamilia, who is getting ready to unleash her magic, but I can’t afford to show my back to these guys who all have the job of knight and have their swords drawn. Their swords are made of mithril of fairly high purity, so I can’t afford to get hit by their attacks.

「Stop it, you fools! Have you forgotten the mission you have been given?」

「Please stay quiet, Commander. Don’t you find it frustrating to simply be on the receiving end of things? Well, maybe it’s a bit much to ask for knightly pride from the Commander, who comes from a commoner background, though.」

「…..」

Apparently, this elderly knight, who is called the commander, is from a commoner background and is unable to lead these guys, who seem to be from a high-ranking nobility background. I think it’s not because he lacks leadership capabilities, but simply because these guys look down on him and won’t listen to what he says. Knights who come from high-ranking noble families from another country, huh. How should I deal with them? While I’m thinking about this, Lunamilia’s magical energy begins to swell. I thought that as expected, if they were exposed to this much magical energy, they would shut up, but it seems they don’t have magical energy perception skill, and don’t seem to notice Lunamilia’s abnormal flow of magical energy.

After a while, a divine aura emanates from Lunamilia. Not good, this is bad. I thought that she would use evil warding arrow or something, but a magic that’s comparable, no, even greater than the superhuman magic she used on the demonic dragon is coming. Even so, the magic activation is too fast.

As Lunamilia’s divine aura begins to overflow, as expected, the knights seem to notice her abnormal state, and they stare at her in shock, at a loss for words. Ugh, I can’t stop my body from shaking and palpating due to the intense killing intent and fear of death. This is bad, I absolutely have to prevent this magic from being activated, no matter what.

「Divine Eradicating….」

「Stop it, Luna!」

「Please wait, Lunamilia-dono!」

The elderly knight and I use instant step to get in front of Lunamilia and stop her from activating the magic. Holy cow, what kind of magic is that?

「Sei-sama….」

「It’s okay, Luna. Look, these guys no longer the will to fight.」

As Lunamilia stops casting her magic, her magical energy and divine aura begin to disappear. It looks like the worst has been averted. The knights are stunned and unable to stand up due to fear, so it should be okay to leave them alone. Lunamilia’s magic just now, the moment I heard the word 「Divine」, it reminded me of the power of the god I met during my reincarnation. I must not make an enemy of Lunamilia, never.

I look at the elderly knight who tried to stop Lunamilia next to me. I’m impressed that he was able to move even as he got exposed to that divine aura, but not only is sweat trickling down his entire face, he has a desperate look.

「Phew, now then, Commander-san. Can you tell us your side of the story?」

「M, mm.」

After calming down, the Commander tells me their purpose. After hearing rumors about the sacred magic, Heavenly Judgement, that Lunamilia used in Astoma, Lambert’s territory, they came here to verify its authenticity on the Pope’s order. Heavenly Judgement is a sacred magic that only the Pope can use, and is said to be used in trials before God to expose false testimony and to increase the prestige of the Pope and the Holy Church. They believed that the outrageous rumor that a young girl who had just become a monk had used it was without a doubt false information, but it was a major job for the knight order of the Holy Kingdom, who usually have nothing to do, and they seemed to get overly enthusiastic.

In the villages they stopped by on the way here, Lunamilia was revered as a saint, so it seems that the purpose of their journey ended up changing to condemning the fake saint halfway through it.

「Still, don’t the knights of the Holy Kingdom train on a regular basis? No matter how you look at it, those guys’ fighting abilities are too poor, don’t you think? Can they make it as knights with that level of abilities?」

「Mm. After all, the Holy Kingdom has had no hostile nations or powers for the past few thousand years. We also sprinkle a large amount of holy water throughout the country, so there are no high-ranked monsters either. As for the Undead Labyrinth, the middle stratums and beyond are simply too dangerous, so no one go that far, in other words, there is neither a purpose nor a need to become stronger.」

In this world where God’s grace is a real deal, there is no power that can stand up to the Holy Church. This is because jobs and skills are given by God. And since there are no enemies, there is no need to get stronger. As a result, there are probably nothing but cocky young master knights in the country.

「So, what are you going to do now?」

「Mm, the divine aura I can sense from Lunamilia-dono, and then the magic from earlier. The rumors are all true, and it is no wonder she is revered as a saint. By order of the Pope, it is my mission to escort Lunamilia-dono to the Holy Kingdom.」

Huh? Don’t joke with me. I’ll take Lunamilia to the Holy Kingdom, so you guys aren’t necessary. There’s no way in hell I’d let Lunamilia travel with those kinds of guys.

「I see, then let’s get going. To the Holy Kingdom. Sei-sama, it looks like we have to say goodbye here.」

「Huh, huh?」

Huh, are you serious? What’s going on here? She’s parting ways with me and heading to the Holy Kingdom with these guys? What manner of change of heart has she gone through?

「Sei-sama, let’s meet again in the Holy Kingdom someday. I will finish all the preparations by then.」

「Huh, y, yeah.」

Preparation? As I’m wondering what she means by that, a squeaking sound pops out from the area around Lunamilia’s womb. By preparation, is it the preparation to carry my child? At the tender age of 16, Lunamilia has just changed jobs to Priest. She is supposed to devote herself to the Holy Kingdom for the rest of her life, so is it even possible for her to get pregnant and give birth? Maybe she has some kind of idea.

Lunamilia and the knights begin to get ready to depart.

「Tch, you fake saint. I’ll definitely expose your true identity on the way. I’ve memorized your face, after all.」

「Fufufu, divine punishment will surely befall heretics that go against God’s will.」

Othniel curses at me and Lunamilia. What an idiot. Putting me aside, to think he would make an enemy of Lunamilia, you can say that’s an act that shows no fear, even of God. For him to be able to say such a line even after being exposed to Lunamilia’s divine aura, talk about reckless, or rather, I guess he’s just an idiot. It’s highly doubtful that he will be able to make it to the Holy Kingdom in one piece.

They take Lunamilia with them and head for the Holy Kingdom. Due to this instantaneous, sudden development, our plans have been thrown far away off the course. Now then, what should I do?

「Maybe I should check out the Demonic Dragon Mountain range. Going to the elven country doesn’t like a bad idea either.」

I turn my horse around and set off further east.

Sei (Kars Amberlius), Age 15, Level 72

Job: Porter

Skills: Fast Learning, Appraisal 4, Automatic Recovery 7, Storage 7, Magical Energy Manipulation 7, Magical Energy Perception 5, Body Manipulation 7, Body Enhancement 7, Material Enhancement 6, The Arts of Lovemaking, Instant Step 5, Instant Movement 4, Throwing 4, Intimidation 2, Swordsmanship 6, Spearmanship 6, Boxing 3, Presence Concealment 3, Presence Detection 4, Fire Magic 3, Wind Magic 3, Earth Magic 2, Water Magic 3, Light Magic 3, Shadow Magic 3, Healing Magic 4

## 142×1 - **Intermission – Part 1**

As she got rocked inside the rattling carriage, Ottilie gazed at the scenery outside with a slightly melancholy feeling. After arriving at the royal capital, she immediately submitted a report on Cotton Clouds’ activities, but was immediately summoned by Narkissia, the current king’s younger sister and founder of Cotton Clouds. The response was just too quick. As expected, it seemed that losing three of their members was unacceptable. All of the members of Cotton Cloud were members of noble families from around the royal capital. Were there any bereaved families who wanted to hear the details of what happened? On top of that, there were too many things to report regarding this mission, such as the state of the Chanortham territory, the beastfolk bandit band, the demonic dragon, the user of incredible sacred magic who was revered as a saint, and the young porter who was skilled in combat and had large storage capacity. It was probably going to be a long talk. After arriving at the mansion, she was led by the butler to the pavilion in the garden.

「Ottilie, good job on completing your mission. I know you must be tired having just arrived at the royal capital, but there’s something I’d like to ask you. I’ll have some tea made. Go ahead and take a seat.」

She had long black hair and serene blue eyes. She had her usual elegance as a member of the royal family and a noblewoman. It didn’t seem like Narkissia was in a bad mood. Well, she was not the kind of person who readily lost her temper, but most of the time, you could never tell what she was thinking, so she was the type of person Ottilie was not very good with.

As she sat down and drank the herbal tea made by the waiting maid, she pondered whether she should report and apologize for the loss of their comrades first, right then and there. That was because until this very moment, she had thought that she had been summoned for that purpose.

「Narkissia-sama, we ended up losing three of our precious comrades. I am very sorry and have no excuses.」

「Ah, it’s fine. If you work as an adventurer, there’s always the possibility that you’ll die, after all. One of them lost in a one-on-one duel against a beastfolk, while the two others died in the battle against a demonic dragon. You’re not to blame.」

Contrary to her expectations, Narkissia didn’t seem to be bothered by the deaths of their comrades. If that was the case, then why she had been summoned; she wondered. Did she want to ask about Lunamilia Tarte Art, the girl who became a priest at the tender age of 16 and was revered as a saint? If not for her, in the worst case, Cotton Clouds might have been wiped out. However, the matter Narkissia asked about was something else.

「So, you said it was Sei the porter, I believe? I want to ask something about him.」

Sei the porter. He hailed from the Holy Kingdom and was Lunamilia’s attendant. His skill with the sword was almost on par with Laura’s, and despite his young age, his storage capacity was 64 barrels. To put it into perspective, he had the same storage capacity as the best porter in the country, who was elderly and had limited mobility. Most porters could only get up to 16 barrels throughout their lives. If you worked as an adventurer, he was someone you would definitely love to get your hands on, so it was only natural that Narkissia was interested in him. Ottilie told her all the information she knew, but it wasn’t like she knew that much about him.

「I see, got it. Can you tell me about his physical characteristics?」

「Physical characteristics, is it?」

「Yes, I want you to tell me everything about him, his height, hair color, eye color, and any other characteristics.」

Although she was unable to grasp Narkissia’s intentions, Ottilie recalled and described Sei’s characteristics to her. He was about 180 cm tall. He had blonde hair and, if memory served her right, blue eyes. Ottilie wondered what was the point of learning such things. Perhaps she was planning to find him and take him as a member of the Cotton Clouds? But if that was the case, she didn’t understand the point of asking about his hair and eye color.

「So, you just parted ways with such a talented porter without doing anything?」

「No, Sei, umm, simply put, got into a lover relationship with Laura. As a condition for continuing this relationship, he must give priority to Cotton Clouds’ requests, so I think we will meet again in the royal capital someday.」

「Laura… Ah, the girl who was recently promoted to a regular member, right? I believe I heard she has been blessed with two children. Sei is still in his teens, no? For him to get into relationship with Laura, who is a married woman with children, rather than Sylphia, who is the same age….」

「Apparently, he and Sylphia had known each other since a long time ago, and were friends. Even when I tried to get information about Sei from Sylphia, I couldn’t get anything from her…」

「He’s acquainted with Sylphia even though he’s from the Holy Kingdom, huh.」

「…..」

Now that she mentioned it, it was indeed a strange story. Not only was Sylphia from the Estorias Kingdom, they had been looking after her in Cotton Clouds since she got the job of Hero at the age of 14. She should have neither connection nor relation with the Holy Kingdom. Was it just a convenient lie when he said he was from the Holy Kingdom? A reason for lying about his origins, in other words…

「That’s it for today. You must be tired, so go home and have a good rest, Ottilie. Sigh, I don’t approve of eavesdropping.」

The slight magical energy and gentle breeze she had been feeling since some time ago. Was it eavesdropping using wind magic? A magnificent magical energy manipulation that would be unperceivable unless you had magical energy perception of high proficiency level. They were a considerably skilled magic user. Someone who would not be reprimanded even if they were to eavesdrop on Narkissia’s conversation, and was skilled in wind magic and magical energy manipulation. Who in the world could it be? Unable to think of anyone who fit the bill, Ottilie stopped thinking about it and left the room. The wind magic had stopped.

「Fufufu, still, a lover relationship with Laura, huh. As he grew up without receiving any love from his mother, I wonder if he yearned for motherly love and came to love older women.」

She got the feeling that Narkissia was saying something behind her, but partly because she was tired, Ottilie hurried home.

「Ottilie, do you have a minute?」

Just as she was about to get on the carriage and head home, someone called out to her. When she looked in the direction of the voice, she saw two beautiful girls standing there, who were young now but would surely grow into women of unmatched beauty in the future.

The one who called out to her was Her Royal Highness Princess Latifani Magzard. Although she had not yet been granted a job, she was hailed as a genius in the way of magic, and rumor had it that she had been receiving never-ending marriage proposals. Latifani often visited Narkissia, a high-level mage, to practice magic. It seemed that she was the one who was eavesdropping earlier.

「How can I help you, Your Highness?」

「Can I have a moment of your time? There is something I would like to talk to you about. This is my best friend, Lilicia.」

Lilicia Ambarlius. She was said to be a genius in the way of the sword, and she heard that she often visited the royal capital to practice with knights using real swords. In the future, after she married and gave birth to an heir, there was a good chance that she would join Cotton Clouds and play an active role in it.

「A talk, is it?」

「Yes, it’s about the porter you said you met.」

In contrast to their smiles, the two’s gazes were sharp, hard to believe that they belonged to young girls, and as she got subjected to those gazes, Ottilie felt a chill run down her spine.

## 142×2 - **Intermission – Part 2**

「Saint-sama, thank you very much.」

「Saint-sama…」

「Saint-sama…」

On the way to the Holy Kingdom, Lunamilia, along with the Knights, stopped by the nearest towns and villages and continued with her volunteer activities, the same as before. She went around treating commoners who couldn’t afford to go to the city and pay a large amount of money to have their injuries or illness treated, either free or charge or in exchange for food and lodging. From time to time, in poor villages that couldn’t afford to hire adventurers, she also took on monster subjugation, which oftentimes made the villagers thankful to her and revere her as a saint.

Although the knights had little combat experience, under the leadership of the experienced commander and with the support of Lunamilia’s sacred magic, they were able to subjugate the monsters, so more and more of the knights began to acknowledge Lunamilia.

「Tch, you fake Saint…」

Even after personally witnessing Lunamilia’s sacred magic and volunteer activities, some of the knights, including Othniel, refused to acknowledge her. The perception that Lunamilia came from a baronial family in a rural area they had never heard of, and that she was a greenhorn, as it had only been two years since she obtained the job of monk, made it difficult for them, who came from high-ranking noble families, to honestly accept her abilities. One of the main reasons was that as priests generally almost never served in the military, they couldn’t gauge how different Lunamilia’s abilities were from those of other priests.

On top of that, as they were made to accompany Lunamilia in her charity works, they always ended up staying in poor towns and villages, and the shabby beds and food provided by the common people were nothing but misery. Just thinking that they would have to spend the night in this small village, where they had accepted a request to exterminate the monsters living in the surrounding area, made anger and killing intent towards Lunamilia well up inside them.

「Hey, you guys, there’s something I’d like to talk to you about.」

After a humble dinner at the village chief’s house – that said, it was the best the villagers could offer – Othniel gathered his comrades and began to have a secret talk. While

While Othniel and the others had to sleep in a large room in the village chief’s house, the commander got a single room, as for Lunamilia, they had arranged a detached house for her. The fact that a commoner and a girl from a low-ranking noble family were receiving better treatment than him was humiliating for Othniel. He was sure that his comrades felt the same way.

「You want to attack Lunamilia?」

「Yeah. Worry not, I just want to scare her a bit.」

He was going to teach this young girl who pretended to be a saint her place. She was a cheeky woman, but on closer look, she had a great face and body. They hadn’t had many opportunities to embrace women these past few days, so on their way to the Holy Kingdom, she would make a perfect partner for venting their sexual desire. If she were to become a violated priestess, surely no one would revere her as a saint anymore. Othniel incited his comrades, but the answer he got was not what he expected.

「The heck are you talking about? Lunamilia is a real saint, you know?」

「Don’t you feel that divine aura, Othniel?」

「Exterminating monsters with the support of sacred magic is, how should I put it, very rewarding.」

「Yeah, yeah, it made me feel truly alive for the first time since the day I became a knight.」

「I’ve had an audience with the Pope too, but you see, that divine aura, it’s even greater than the Pope’s. Cease your stupid ideas, Othniel.」

One after another, his comrades acknowledged and praised Lunamilia. Othniel was stunned and at a loss for words at the change in his comrades who, until just a few days ago, had sworn to condemn the fake saint together with him. Killing intent towards Lunamilia, who had deceived them, began to gush out inside him.

As the night drew on, everyone was sleeping like logs, breathing peacefully in their sleep. The long-distance travel and monster extermination, which they were not used to, they did during the day consumed a large amount of stamina, so it was only natural.

「Hey, let’s go.」

In order to launch a night raid on Lunamilia, Othniel slipped out of the room, taking with him two people who, like himself, were growing more and more distrustful of that woman.

「Hey, Othniel, let me do it first, okay?」

「Hehehe, to think we’ll get to have sex with that fake saint of a woman.」

It seemed that these two didn’t really hate Lunamilia like he did, but only thought about raping her. Well, that was also fine. In order to get the better of that cheeky woman, the cooperation of those two was necessary. One person held her down, one person covered her mouth, and one person raped her. Even if the crime came to light, it was nothing to worry about. Not only would it be easy to cover it up by using the power of the families they come from, in the first place, they had never heard of a case where a priestess who served God came forward to say that she had been raped. There was no choice but to suck it up.

Othniel and the others arrive in front of the detached house where Lunamilia was staying. Light was leaking through the gap in the door. It appeared that the room was illuminated by the lighting of light magic or a magic tool. They didn’t expect her to be up this late at night. What should they do, wait for that woman to fall asleep? However, the night temperature was so low that simply being there was torturous. Well, ultimately, the other party was just a single young girl, so they could just cover her mouth. Othniel boldly entered the detached house. It seemed that the door was carelessly left unlocked. What came into view was the figure of Lunamilia sitting in a chair facing them. Could it be that she was waiting for them? Maybe one of his comrades was concerned about Lunamilia’s safety and tattled on him.

「Fufufu, I knew you would come. The malice I felt from you today was stronger than usual, after all.」

「What?」

Lunamilia’s face, faintly illuminated by the lighting tool, was beautiful yet eerie. Perhaps it was light magic, but apart from the lighting tool, Lunamilia herself appeared to be glowing white. More importantly, she said she expected them to come?! Was Lunamilia implying that she could read people’s minds? No, she was a fake saint, a con artist. She might be able to fool everyone, but not him. However, it seemed that his two comrades had ended up getting cold feet.

「H, hey, Othniel. There’s something dangerous about that woman.」

「S, she’s glowing. That’s divine aura, right?! As expected, she must be a real saint…」

「Don’t be afraid, that’s just light magic. She’s not a saint or anything. She’s a con artist, skilled at reading people’s minds, and a user of light magic.」

Lunamilia, who had sensed Othniel’s malice, had already finished the preparation to activate her magic. A torrent of magical energy surged, but Othniel and the others, who didn’t have magical energy perception skill, didn’t notice it. However, they began to feel a strong sense of urgency that something out of the ordinary was looming over them.

「No more talks. You guys, let’s do it.」

「Huh, yeah.」

「S, sure.」

With Othniel in the lead, the three of them charged at Lunamilia. However, their path ended up blocked by something divine that was emanating from Lunamilia. This was light magic, and was nothing more than a blind. Light magic should have no offensive power. However, perhaps out of fear, the three were shaking and unable to move any further.

「Divine Ascension」

Lunamilia’s sacred magic was activated. As a vortex of divine energy engulfed the sky above the entire village, Othniel and the others felt a strange sensation in the area around their chests and held them down with both hands.

「Ugh, this, what have you done, you fake saint?!」

「My chest, my chest is…」

「Uwaaahhhh」

Othniel and the others fell to their knees and began to suffer. A short while after, a white mist-like object shot out from the chests of the three of them, slowly rising through the ceiling and into the sky.

「…..」

Othniel and the others were silently, absentmindedly staring into space with unfocused eyes, drool dripping from their mouths. What was left behind there was nothing but three flesh puppets with beating hearts.

「Lunamilia-dono, is something the matter? Ugh, this is…」

The commander, who sensed the intense divine aura and magical energy, visited Lunamilia’s room. What he saw there was the figures of the three who had completely changed. These three were the people who stubbornly refused to acknowledge Lunamilia. Judging from the situation, it seemed that the three had sneaked into Lunamilia’s bedroom and tried to commit an assault, but ended up having the tables turned on them. However, the unusual state of the three. What on earth had happened?

「Knight Commander, it seems that the Holy Kingdom is full of corrupt people like them, who blaspheme God and live according to their desires, with only their family background as their sole redeeming feature. I have to purge them and build a kingdom that is truly devoted to God. Will you cooperate with me?」

「Y, yes, Lunamilia-sama.」

Exposed to Lunamilia’s intense divine aura, the Knight Commander quickly replied. For a moment, he thought, 「Shoot」, in regret. Lies didn’t work on Lunamilia. As she was a user of Heavenly Judgment, which condemned those who lied to her, lying to her meant death. However, he quickly reconsidered. In the Holy Kingdom, family background was everything, and regardless of how much he devoted himself to the country, he ended up getting looked down upon even by his subordinates simply because he was from a commoner background. The details of what Lunamilia was trying to do were unknown, but he could sympathize with what she was saying. He thought believing in the extraordinary divine aura that emanated from her and pledging allegiance to her would not be a bad idea either.

「Lunamilia-sama, I apologize for my subordinates intruding upon you so late in the night. Hey, you guys, let’s go back.」

「…..」

Othniel and the others silently listened to the Commander’s instructions and then went back unsteadily. The change, as if they had turned into living corpses, and the sacred magic that Lunamilia had activated. The Knight Commander took what he had just seen to heart and decided to go to bed. Not long after they returned to the Holy Kingdom, similar phenomenon would occur over and over again, mainly on those from high-ranking noble families, but that was a story for another time.

「As I thought, it was the right choice to part ways with Sei-sama. I can’t afford to let God spend time with such unbelievers, after all. Fufufu, Sei-sama, until the day we meet again, I will transform the Holy Kingdom into a country worthy of you, and finish the preparation to be blessed with the child of God.」

## 143 - **Onward to the East**

At the foot of the demonic dragon mountain range, a great sword and a giant battle axe clash against each other, and along with a metallic sound, a shockwave of thunder and flames spread throughout the surrounding area.

A lightning-clad divine steel sword and a scorching flame-emitting demonic battle axe are swung around with a thunderous roar, and simply getting close to them causes low-ranking monsters to instantly be reduced to corpses. Monsters that are sensitive to magical energy and strength seem to have made themselves scarce from the surrounding area.

The strongest in the kingdom versus the strongest in the empire. The difference in strength between those two and me is clear, and just getting close to them is fatal to me, who has low magical defense, as I will be hit by lightning and flames. If I value my life, I should leave this place at once. However, I have a reason to stay here. It’s not because the one who is currently fighting is my cousin. It’s for my own sake. I probably only have one chance. The fact that I have the Flame Salamander Bracelet and a full set of Demonic Dragon armor, which have fire magic resistance, with me is reassuring.

I conceal my presence and hide myself in the bushes. Bakumada, the great general of the Carcas Empire, is an incredibly high-level mad warrior, boasting an extraordinary level of defense when using body enhancement, and perhaps out of confidence, he doesn’t seem to be wary of his surrounding area at all. There should be an opportunity I can take advantage of.

I am missing my left arm and right eye, so I wonder if I will be able to move well. No, I have no choice but to do it. In order to continue my adventuring activities, I have no choice but to do it.

The battle between these two, who boast superhuman strength, is reaching its climax. Here it is!
